 ) The famous '360 Modena Ferrari', which was once Sachin Tendulkar's ride, has been bought by a Surat businessman

 do maheene chali gahan jaanch ke baad do alag-alag vyaktiyon par aarope laga

 ) uttar pradesh kaa mukhyamantri koun hoga ise lekar bijepi kisi bhi naam par abhi tak mohar nahin laga paaya he
 The BJP decides the Chief Minister as part of its strategy
 aksar aisa dekha gaya he chunaav se pehle bijepi apane mukhyamantri ke naam kii ghoshnaa nahin karata he
 But in the last, an anonymous leader becomes the Chief Minister, which has probably never been discussed in the media before
 aisa jharkhand or haryana main bhi ho chukaa he, kya aisa is baar bhi uttar pradesh main hoga? chaahe jo bhi mukhyamantri bane lekin sabase dilachasp baat yah he ki sutara ke hawaale se whatsap par kai netaa mukhyamantri ban gaye he
 Every hour a new face is coming out and it is written in it that the source has revealed that this leader is going to become the next Chief Minister of Uttar Pradesh
 agar whatrup kii maani jaae to uttar pradesh main das se bhi zyada naam mukhyamantri ke liye charchaa main he or un main se kuch naam 'shortlist' bhi ho chuke hai
 After the resounding victory in Uttar Pradesh, the four names of the BJP who were the most talked about in the media for the Chief Minister are Manoj Sinha, Dinesh Sharma, Keshav Prasad Maurya, Shrikant Sharma
 kuch din tak in naamon par kaaphi charchaa hui
 Meanwhile, Keshav Prasad Maurya's health deteriorated and he had to be hospitalized
 isse pehle amit shah ne yah elaan kar diya ki keshav prasad maury hi tay karenge koun hoga uttarapradesh kaa aglaa mukhyamantri
 Then came the news that Maurya is all right and this routine is checked up
 chunaav vyastata kii vajah se thodaa blad pressure badha hua he
 Whether it is due to blood pressure or something else, it is proved by Amit Shah's statement that there is little chance of Maurya becoming Chief Minister
 lagata nahin ki maury khud apana naam mukhyamantri ke rup main aage badhayenge
 Then after a while, a new name now appears in whatsapp and that is Home Minister Rajnath Singh
 nattejey ke baad rajnath singh kaa naam kabhi bhi mukhyamantri ke rup main charchaa main nahin tha lekin whatsap par yah sandesh failana laga ki rajnath singh uttar pradesh ke agle mukhyamantri honge
 It was also reported that the staff of Rajnath Singh have also reached Lucknow and preparations have started
 sirf itnaa nahin whatsap main yah bhi sandesh aane laga ki rajnath ke jane ke baad ab grahamantri kaa bhaar arun jetali sanbhaalenge or piyush goyal vittamantri honge
 But no such formal announcement has been made by the BJP
 tippaniyan After some time another name comes up in the discussion - Satish Mahana, a seven-time MLA from Kanpur
 yah bhi charchaa hui ki mahana ko dilli bulaayaa gaya or unki mulaakaat pradhanmantri narendra modi or bijepi adhyaksh amit shah se hui

 phir sutara ke hawaale se whatsap par dinesh sharma kaa naam aayaa

 phir ek saathi bataate he ki ek jyotish ne bataaya he ki koi mahila netaa mukhyamantri banegi or vah smriti irani he or smriti somnath mandir darshan karne bhi gayi he
 All these names are running on whatsapp quoting the sutra
 ab aap khud tay kar lijie mukhyamantri koun banegaa

 uttar pradesh main shandaar jeet ke baad bijepi kii taraf se jo chaar naam mukhyamantri ke liye media main sabase zyada charchaa main the ve hai manoj sinha, dinesh sharma, keshav prasad maury, shrikant sharma

 is bich keshav prasad maury kii tabiyat karaab ho gai or unhen aspataal main bhartee karwaanaa padaa
 Earlier, Amit Shah announced that Keshav Prasad Maurya will decide who will be the next Chief Minister of Uttar Pradesh
 phir khabar ai ki maury bilkul thik hai or yah routine check ap he

 chaahe blad pressure kii vajah se ho yaa kuch or amit shah ke bayaan se yah to sabit ho gaya ki maury ke mukhyamantri banane kaa chance bahut kam he

 phir kuch der ke baad whatsap main ab ek nayaa naam saamne aata he or vah he grahamantri rajnath singh

 He captained India for a decade but his career was marred after he was banned on match-fixing allegations
 He appealed against the life ban and recently the Andhra Pradesh High Court lifted the life ban on him
 He made his foray into politics by joining the Congress party in 2009 and is now an MP
